 kisaanon kii madad karne ke liye desh main sahakaari bank hai
 He reaches out to the smallest farmers in the country at a time when he is most in need of cash
 apane khet main buaai ke liye
 It is very easy to do math
 Cooperative banks usually give loans up to Rs 46,000 for sowing certain crops in one hectare field
 is ek hectare par khadi kii gai fasal kisaan ko lagbhag 1 lakh rupee tak kamakar detii he
 The farmer makes a profit of about Rs 54,000 per hectare by returning the loan amount of Rs 46,000 from his total income
 khet se bazaar takkooparative bank se karj lekar kheti karne ke baad jaise hi kisaan kii fasal katane or bikne ke liye taiyaar hoti he uski chunauti fasal ke liye uchit graahak khojane kii rahati he
 The farmer usually gets a chance to sell his crop at the support price fixed by the government
 lekin yahaan maujuud sahakaari bank kisaan kii ek lakh rupee kii cell se apane karj kaa 46,000 rupee kaat lete hai
 54,000 is saved by selling the crop in the hands of the farmer
 lihaaja, kah len ki karj lekar kheti karne main kisaan ke paas sirf aadhi kamai bachati he
 Not a serious loan; In farmers' cooperative mandis, the farmer only gets half of the earnings of the crop if he sells the crop under the supervision of the cooperative bank
 lihaaja zyaadaatar kisaan in sahakaari mandiyon par nunatam samarthan mulya par apni fasal bechney se kataraate hai
 In such a situation, the farmers extract their profits by giving their crop to the middlemen sitting in the market at a paltry price (60 to 70 thousand rupees)
 nateeja, karj ko syriasli nahin lene se kisaanon ko prati hectare apni kamai main ijapha karne kaa mauka mil jaataa he
 Now what will happen to the loan? After taking loan for sowing from the bank, the farmer surrenders the crop to the cooperative mandis, not to sell the crop to increase his earnings
 aisa karne se kisaan ko adhik munafa ho jate hai jabaki use kooparative mandiyon se kam dar par apni fasal bechni padati he
 Apart from this, to sell the crop on the market, the farmers have to transport the crop to the market at their own cost
 saath hi use mandi main kai dinon tak fasal bikne kaa intjaar bhi karnaa padataa he
 The farmers wait for elections, after the crop is sold in Mandi, where the farmer gets paid after deducting the debt, he is not expected to get cash also
 aam taur par kooparative bank kisaan ke munaafe kii rakam kaa draft yaa check banaakar jari karte hai
 Hence, they get cash after 15-20 days of selling the crop
 in dikkaton se bachane ke liye kisaan bichauliyon par zyada bharosa isliye karata he kyonki uske haath main adhik paisa aane ke saath-saath use fasal kaa sauda karte hue puraa paisa cash main mil jaataa he
